< Text>
The Onyx Club had been under investigation since November when Roseville police say they got a tip that bar staff were involved in narcotics sales while working.
Undercover agents with Roseville police and the Department of Alcoholic Beverage Control were able to buy cocaine. Several violations were documented, police say.

As a result of the investigation, the bar‚Äôs ownership has agreed to several penalties, including: a 30-day suspension (beginning on Jan. 3, 2019), three year suspended revocation, limitations of alcohol sales to the patio after 10 p.m. from Sunday through Wednesday and 1 a.m. Thursday through Saturday, and the hiring of one licensed and uniformed security guard on Fridays and Saturdays.</Text>

< Review>
I really loved my quesadilla!! The carne asada -real steak - was cooked perfect. I put rice in mine and the rice was fluffy just the way mom used to make it. Enough cheese...just right amount and with ¬πoinons and cilantro. The other nice touch was the salsa - no not pace picante factory made stuff - the delicious home made flavors - the right heat too. I like it hot but not where my lips go numb.
My partner had a breakfast burrito - beans/refried, onions, cilantro, bacon and egg. All cooked right not overcooked egg.
A hole in the wall off the main road. Actually it was on the historic route 66. But i didnt know that and the directions didnt say so.
The place was small 1 person running the orders inside and on the phone. I thought ooh ooh its could be a long wait but, we got our food rather quickly. The seats were torn in places and the place wasn't detailed clean but it was tidy and no trash on floor or dirty tables. So that was cool with me. The lady that took our order was smiling and spoke english very well. Very nice to everyone in there.
I gave this 4 stars because there was room for improvement. But i am looking forward to my return to Laughlin and I'll be SURE to stop over in Needles at Munich's there again!!! 5 star delish.
No vegan.except rice and beans - complete protein -and tortillas, bell pepper, onions, tomatoes and cilantro.
Go get ya some!</Review>

< text>
This place is really different for a Sacramento bar. It gives me a feel of unique "snug" places you get in New York. And to top it off, the Penicillin is untouchable here! Hands down 1 of the best Penicillins I've had.

My only complaint (as my fam and I have come here ALOT) was that the service was really bad a certain night at the bar. Pretty disappointed in the racial profiling. Lindsay and Tony- who are known as great bartenders- provided no service as we sat there. Lindsay ignored us and helped other customers that came up to the bar after us. Eventually we found seating else where and got serviced by Carrie- who made up for the lack of customer service from them. You should be aware of how you treat your customers.< /text>
